 (* Write a  function to check whether any value in a sequence exists in a sequence or not. *)
let rec seq_exists seq =
  match seq with
  | [] -> false
  | _ ->
      let rec seq_exists seq =
        match seq with
        | [] -> false
        | x ->
            let rec seq_exists seq =
              match seq with
              | [] -> false
              | x ->
                  if x = seq then true
                  else seq_exists (seq - x)
            in
            seq_exists seq
      in
      seq_exists seq

 (* Write a  function to check whether any value in a sequence exists in a sequence or not. *)
let rec seq_exists seq =
  match seq with
  | [] -> false
  | _ ->
      let rec seq_exists seq =
        match seq with
        | [] -> false
        | x ->
            let rec seq_exists seq =
              match seq with
              | [] -> false
              | x ->
                  if x = seq then true
                  else seq_exists (seq - x)
            in
            seq_exists seq
      in
      seq_exists seq
